FNV PPLIGHTING B-RANGE CONSTRUCTOR +0xDC DEEP AUDIT

Questions:
1. Does FUN_00B66F50 construct the object whose vtable contains BDB4A0/BDF790?
2. Which vtable immediate does FUN_00B66F50 assign, if any?
3. Are +0xDC setter/copy/destructor helpers near B66F50 part of the same object type?
4. Do texture slot setters B66640/B68660 connect source texture slots to draw-time PPLighting stages?
5. What is the role of the extra BD9D00 caller FUN_00BC3E40?
